To achieve net zero energy, we’re convinced the world needs new business models and applications, not only science and engineering. \n\nOur mission stems from three core beliefs:\n\n#### Global CO2 footprint awareness is driving behaviour change\n\nFossil fuels cause 76% of global emissions. Business as usual is no longer viable\n\n#### We have the technology needed to go carbon-free\n\nVisionary products and services that spark a mass adoption of existing renewables is what we need now\n\n#### Digital companies utilising data create the most value\n\nThe digital layer that balances, orchestrates and leverages physical infrastructure is the area of value\n\n#### Energy causes 76% of all CO2 emissions. Have a solution?\n\n[Pitch it to us](https://setventures.com/share-your-pitchdeck/) \n\n##### What we look for\n\nWe back Europe’s innovative energy entrepreneurs. We believe in the people behind great ideas. That's why we are in the business-building business, not the “deal” or “capital” business. Together with our experienced partners we have a track record of leveraging relationships to build teams, attract partners and customers and then–together–build successful businesses.We are active partners who do everything we can for our companies and have not forgotten how to hustle. Your company is like a gun. Take care that it is always LOADED. LOADED.VENTURES brings you - good advice - perfect partners - growth potential. Don't join us. We will join you. We love to co-invest in businesses that change the game. We love to start-up start-ups en to help existing business grow. We prefer to be actively involved in the fields of healthy and functional food, sustainable companies and tech. Door vraag en aanbod te verbinden en dit te ondersteunen met informatie en onafhankelijk advies ontstaan nieuwe kansen.\n\n[Bekijk hoe](https://venturecapital.nl/marktplaats/) \n\n## Op zoek naar Venture Capital?\n\nVentureCapital.nl / PrivateEquity.nl is het platform dat vraag en aanbod bij elkaar brengt. Ontstaan uit het idee om de investeerdersmarkt transparanter te maken door vraag en aanbod via internet te ontsluiten. Plaats, als ondernemer of investeerder, vrijblijvend een profiel. Interesse via het platform of vanuit ons netwerk sturen wij één op één door zodat je makkelijk en snel contact kan opnemen met de geïnteresseerde investeerder(s). Het platform werkt eenvoudig en snel, met een eenmalige listing fee, zodat je op een [goedkope manier in contact komt met investeerders](https://venturecapital.nl/pakket-kiezen/). Het is volledig gericht op de ‘matchmaking’ in Nederland.\n\n[Vind kansen](#2) \n\n![Venture Capital Nederland](https://venturecapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2023/10/Venture-Capital-Nederland.jpg \"Venture Capital Nederland\") \n\n\n\n## Durfkapitaal vinden\n\nBen je met jouw bedrijf op zoek naar durfkapitaal en wil je op transparante wijze verbonden worden aan een investeerder waar je wat aan hebt? Plaats dan een investeringsprofiel en wij helpen je bij de eerst volgende stap.\n\n[Bedrijfsprofiel plaatsen](https://venturecapital.nl/ondernemers) \n\n\n\n## Vraag en aanbod markt\n\nBekijk onze vraag en aanbod. Neem een kijkje in het type ondernemers en investeerders die wij huisvesten binnen ons netwerk. Zit jouw match er tussen of wil je meer informatie dan helpen wij je graag met onafhankelijk goed advies.\n\n[Bekijk vraag en aanbod](https://venturecapital.nl/marktplaats) \n\n\n\n## Investeringskansen\n\nInformatie (zoals [Wat is Venture Capital?](https://venturecapital.nl/wat-is-een-venture-capitalist/)) en investeringskansen zijn op het platform terug te vinden. Wil jij slim je geld investeren in bedrijven of personen zonder veel tijd te verspillen aan de rotte appels? Door een zoekprofiel te plaatsen helpen jou met het vinden van de juiste investering. \n\n[Zoekprofiel opstellen](https://venturecapital.nl/investeerders) \n\n## Uitgelicht Ga hiervoor naar “[Ondernemers](https://venturecapital.nl/ondernemers/)” of “[Investeerders](https://venturecapital.nl/investeerders/)”.\n\n**Waarom is het plaatsen van vraag op VentureCapital.nl gratis?**  \nVentureCapital.nl wil de markt van Venture Capital / Private Equity transparanter en toegankelijker maken en maakt plaatsing van vraag daarom zo laagdrempelig mogelijk. Voor ook het [vraag en aanbod van venture capital](https://venturecapital.nl/marktplaats/).\n\n**Is het plaatsen van profielen echt zo goedkoop?**  \nJa, het plaatsen van profielen is op basis van een [listingsfee](https://venturecapital.nl/pakket-kiezen/) en zonder succesfee of andere verrassingen achteraf. Dit omdat we middels het platform plaatsing zo laagdrempelig en toegankelijk mogelijk willen maken voor zowel ondernemers als investeerders.\n\n**Is het mogelijk om als extern bedrijf te adverteren op VentureCapital.nl / PrivateEquity.nl?**  \nJa, dit is zeker mogelijk. Zie hiervoor de [advertentie informatie](https://venturecapital.nl/adverteren/).\n\n## **Venture Capital Partners**\n\nHeb je hulp nodig bij het fundraise traject, bijvoorbeeld bij het waarderen van een onderneming waarin je wilt investeren, of bij de beoordeling/opstellen van investeringsovereenkomsten? Wij werken samen met diverse partners die je tijdens het financieringsproces kunnen bijstaan.\n\nBekijk hier de [partners](https://venturecapital.nl/partners) van VentureCapital.nl en neem vrijblijvend contact met ze op.\n\n[![Venture capital partner](https://venturecapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Tiger-logo.png \"Venture capital company founded in 2012\\. We invest in growing companies with a profitable core business that use technology as a differentiator. Vortex has applied an active approach since inception combining operating experience with investment know-how. As a result, our team today is a mix of senior executives, business operators and investment professionals. Thus far Vortex has invested in 26 companies with more than 70 add-on aquisitions.\n\nWe enjoy to support entrepreneurs and management teams who are committed to building leading companies. We operate as one team to ensure that the right strategy, structure and support are in place. Together with management we invest in the next level of sustainable growth and providing support when needed.\n\nVortex facilitates buyouts and can provide growth capital as part of a buyout transaction. Our focus is on companies with headquarters in Belgium or in the Netherlands.\n\n## Technology to enable efficient growth\n\n(Information) Technology is key to grow effeciently and to build a sustainable competitive advantage. With our inhouse technology expertise, we can support companies to further align IT and Technology with the business strategy, including buy or build decisions, hiring tech talent and by advising on roadmaps and IT investments.\n\n## Experienced team of investment professionals and business operators\n\nWe are a seasoned team combining many years of m&a experience with deep technical expertise and first hand experience of leading businesses. We consider ourselves active investors while not taking over the steering wheel from management. To support our companies, we tap into our own team and an extended network of experts and strategic partners.\n\nOur mutual drive to build successful businesses has led to a strong track record and substantial value creation.\n\n[ Meet the team ](/team/) \n\n**Experienced team of transaction and portfolio management professionals**\n\nWe are a seasoned team combining many years of m&a experience with deep technical expertise and first hand experience of founding and scaling businesses. We consider ourselves active investors while not taking over the steering wheel from management. People describe us as pragmatic, business savy and accessible. To support our companies, we bring a network of experts and strategic partners. Our mutual drive to build successful businesses has led to a strong track record and above average returns for the shareholders.\n\n[ Meet the team ](/team/) \n\n**IT and Technology to enable efficient growth**\n\nTechnology and IT is an important enabler for businesses to grow effeciently and to build a sustainable competitive advantage.  \nWith our inhouse technology expertise we help companies to align IT/Technology with the business strategy (incl. buy or build decisions, tech team set-up, technology investments levels)\n\n##  The Vortex team\n\n### Evert Jan de Groot\n\nPartner\n\n### Joost Moerland\n\nPartner\n\n### Jorre Bonjer\n\nOperating partner\n\n### Dalip Dewan\n\nOperating partner\n\n### Thomas Fleischer\n\nInvestment Manager\n\n### Agnes Wietrzyk\n\nInvestment Manager\n\n### Jeroen de Vreede\n\nInvestment Manager\n\n### Robert Ernst\n\nAssociate\n\n### Kelsey Tanner\n\nDirector Finance & ESG\n\n### Deron Amen\n\nInvestment manager\n\n### Rick Jan de Vries\n\nAnalyst\n\n[ Meet the whole team ](/team/) \n\n## Case study\n\nNext case study \n\nTogether with Vortex, we saw an opportunity for the creation of a one-stop shop for mission-critical IT services within the SME segment. This proved to be an extremely successful strategy in the Netherlands, and with our scalable platform, we are looking forward to continuing this journey abroad.\n\n**Barry Wissink, CEO hallo,**\n\n[](/portfolio/mascus/) \n\nAt Cars-on-the-web (now Adesa Europe), we saw the opportunity to become the leading portal for used cars in the B2B segment in Europe. Since day 1, we were on the same page with Vortex. We were able to accelerate growth by defining clear priorities, having financial muscle to invest and by solving our key technology challenges. Acquiring German competitor GW Liste marked a step change in our growth journey and relevance in Europe. Vortex played a pivotal role to prepare and sell the business to KAR, a US based strategic owner.\n\n**Johan Meyssen – CEO at Adesa Europe**\n\n[](/portfolio/cars-on-the-web/) \n\nTogether we disentangled Mascus from its parent company, a stock listed publishing company Alma Media. Mascus is a global online marketplace for buying and selling trucks and heavy machinery. We turned Mascus into a stand-alone business with a dedicated international team allowing it to start growing again. The organic growth and the various add-on acquisitions contributed to Mascus being the undisputed leader for advertising heavy machinery equipment. The acquisition by Ritchie Bros. in 2016 is a testament to what the team has accomplished, a great step for Mascus and something I am really proud of.\n\n**Tim Scholte – CEO Mascus (part of Ritchie Bros. Dat vraagt om toewijding, geduld en kapitaal. Maar dat vraagt vooral om ondernemers. Echte ondernemers met echt goede plannen voor het Nederland van de toekomst. En wij zijn er om die echt goede plannen te financieren. Wij zijn Invest-NL, impact investors. Wij maken morgen mogelijk. Prettig kennis te maken.\n\n[Meer over ons](/over-ons?lang=nl \"Over ons\")\n\n### \n\n\\*Het door Invest-NL gecommitteerde kapitaal verwijst naar de hoeveelheid geld die Invest-NL bruto sinds het begin van zijn bestaan heeft toegezegd te investeren in verschillende projecten, ondernemingen of financiële instrumenten.\n\n### Laatste nieuws\n\n### \n\n### Verhalen\n\n### Op zoek naar financiering?\n\nMet enkele korte, gerichte vragen schatten wij in of jouw project of onderneming in aanmerking komt. Active as hands-on investor since 2005 with a wide network of technology experts.\n\n# We build great technology companies\n\nValue Creation Capital is an investing entrepreneur in Deep Tech. Active as hands-on investor since 2005 with a wide network of technology experts.\n\n[read more](#scrollto%5F2)\n\n### What we look for\n\n## Deep Tech companies targeting B2B markets, both start- and scale-ups. Value Creation Capital provides seed capital and series A funding.\n\nWe are specialized in Deep Tech, more specifically in the field of medical devices and analysis, industry 5.0, GRC including cyber security and quantum infrastructure.\n\nWe support ambitious Deep Tech start-ups and scale-ups with seed and growth funding.\n\nWe focus on start-ups in and around the Netherlands and scale-ups in Western Europe.\n\n#### Do you fit our profile?\n\n[Pitch us](https://www.vcxc.com/pitch-us/)\n\n### Our portfolio and our exits\n\n## Since 2005 VCC has very successfully invested in 40+ tech companies with a focus on AI software and High-Tech.\n\n[ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/indica/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/optics11/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/delmic/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/sceptr/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/dispertech/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/amsterdam-scientific-instruments/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/measureworks/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/fastmicro/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/fizyr/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/basetime/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/20face/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/inprocess-lsp/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/cryo-cloud/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/confocal-nl/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/mmox/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/optics11-life/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/ureason/) [ ](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/item/capptions/)\n\n#### Meet more companies\n\n[Our portfolio](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/our-companies/) [Exits](https://www.vcxc.com/portfolio/exits/)\n\n### Our impact\n\nOur mission is simple: we build great technology companies that have a **significant impact on society**. Through key enabling technologies like Optics & Photonics, Nano technology, Robotics, Extended Reality, Advanced sensoring and AI software, we focus on three key societal themes: Healthy Life, Energy and Materials reduction and Security & Safety. Join us in shaping a future where technology not only advances, but also enhances the fabric of our society.\n\n### Our approach\n\nWe have a **clear and fast process** for assessing our future relationships. We support you on **10 processes** that create value with our building blocks.\n\n#### Want to know more?\n\n[Read more](https://www.vcxc.com/approach/our-beliefs/)\n\n**We know that building a tech company is a tough journey**. on dealflow  \n\nAbout Venture IQ\n\n## Empower your team with data-driven insights\n\nVenture IQ empowers M&A, investment, and innovation teams with data-driven insights. With AI, smart automation and human expertise, we help you **find, understand and close more deals**, saving you time filtering through the noise. Venture IQ enables your team to focus on the deals that matter and confidently take action, knowing the context and complete market landscape.\n\n[Learn more![Read More Arrow-icon](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/60e41d6417067c183650597e_next%20(1).svg)](/services)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64f9dcbccf039a1529087b09_Screen-2.webp)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64f9dcbceeca041dd8dce7a7_Screen-1.webp)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64fa1f51d97db8cd45bc221d_Cutout-1.webp)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64fa227e2323abc67345e1fc_Screen-Raised-Funding.webp)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64fa227e2077f1f3c0a66e0c_Screen-Growth.webp)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64fa227e2323abc67345e205_Screen-Financials.webp)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64fa22076cd56b474af3a1d1_Screen-3.webp)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60e41d6417067c5f6b5058ee/64fa21b08589b5ac049dbd0d_Cutout-2.webp)\n\nServices\n\n## Discover and understand companies in any industry  \n\nWhether your team is looking for startups, SMEs, or established companies, Venture IQ's experts help you identify more opportunities across any geography or market. ones](https://www.henq.vc/#portfolio)\n\n[![Approach](https://www.henq.vc/assets/henq/img/btns/arrow-down.svg)](#approach)\n\n## Approach\n\n### \n\n## Approach\n\nWe like any **early stage** B2B software business that is simply a little **different**, whether your market is considered “too **boring**” by some, your business model a little **atypical**, or your founder-passion bordering on **obsession**.\n\n## Before we invest\n\n ↔\n\nConversation about things you actually care about.\n\n✍🏻\n\nNo need to build decks or investor pleasing models, we work with the documents and metrics that you use to steer the business.\n\n📅\n\nDays rather than weeks between first meeting & signed term sheet. The market may change its pace, we never do.\n\n## After we invest\n\n🎯\n\nDeeply committed investor that aims for a 100% hit rate: no spray and pray with us, you will be 1 of the 3 companies we invest in each year.\n\n🤷🏽‍♀️\n\nA shareholder that dares to say “I don’t know” and lets you run the business in the way you see fit. No pushing for influence or of bad ideas.\n\n🔥\n\nWhen we do something, we do it well: the best support in hiring, fundraising & target setting.\n\n## \n\n📌\n\nhenQvc companies use **less funding** and **dilute less** to grow to 10M ARR / annualized net revenue than the average VC backed business.\n\n💸\n\nWe are fine if you want to build a **sustainable business** without ever raising VC funding again. If you do decide to raise: as a henQ portfolio company your chances of raising a proper follow-on round are **2,7x** better than the market average.\n\n## Portfolio\n\nhenQ invests in founders rather than markets. We never back a company that competes with one of our own. [](https://hollandcapital.nl/en/)\n\nSelecteer een pagina \n\nWaardecreatie  \nin venture, growth  \nen buy-out\n\n[PORTFOLIO](https://hollandcapital.nl/portfolio/)[STRATEGIE](https://hollandcapital.nl/strategie/) \n\n[7](#Tekst \"team Holland Capital\") \n\n# **Technologie**\n\nHolland Capital richt zich op het ondersteunen van groei in bedrijven met technologieën die substantiële economische impact hebben binnen de fondstermijn. Deze technologieën zorgen ervoor dat bestaande activiteiten efficiënter worden uitgevoerd, en soms ontstaan er zelfs complete nieuwe economische activiteiten. Holland Capital richt zich op de volgende sectoren: mobiel, software & cloud, data infrastructuur, data analytics, internet of things, cyber security.\n\nDeze strategische benadering positioneert Holland Capital als een belangrijke speler in het investeringslandschap, met een toewijding aan het ondersteunen en koesteren van bedrijven die technologische vooruitgang stimuleren. De toewijding van het bedrijf aan bedrijven die belangrijke economische bijdragen leveren wordt weerspiegeld in haar investeringsstrategieën. Door bedrijven in de voorhoede van technologische innovatie te identificeren en met hen samen te werken, wil Holland Capital niet alleen rendement genereren voor zijn investeerders, maar ook bijdragen aan het bredere economische landschap. Deze toekomstgerichte benadering sluit aan bij het voortdurend veranderende karakter van de technologie-industrie. Holland Capital zoekt naar mogelijkheden waar technologische vooruitgang niet alleen de groei van de bedrijven waarin wordt geïnvesteerd stimuleert, maar ook bijdraagt aan de algehele economische ontwikkeling en vooruitgang, lees ook meer over [Claude kondigt Nederlandse clubtour aan](https://nllife.news/claude-kondigt-nederlandse-clubtour-aan/).\n\n# **Healthcare**\n\nOm de kwaliteit van de zorg te verbeteren en de groei van de zorguitgaven te beperken is ondernemerschap en innovatie cruciaal. Holland Capital investeert in innovatieve zorgondernemers die een langdurige impact in de zorg willen realiseren en die beschikken over kennis van zorgprocessen, implementatiekracht en bovenal doorzettingsvermogen. Onze focus ligt hierbij op aanbieders van healthcare services, medical devices, diagnostics en digital health.\n\n# **Agrifood**\n\nVanuit onze ervaringen in de Technologie en Healthcare sectoren zien we grote kansen in de Agrifood tech sector. Technologie speelt een steeds grotere rol o.a. om yields en productiviteit te verhogen en om negatieve impact activiteiten te minimaliseren. Daarnaast speelt voeding een steeds belangrijkere rol in de preventie van ziektes en bij het naleven van een gezonde levensstijl.\n\n### Assets under management\n\n### Founded\n\n### Investments\n\n### Offices\n\n### Team members\n\n# **Ervaren & hands-on**\n\nHolland Capital is één van de eerste onafhankelijke participatiemaatschappijen in Nederland. Wij investeren al meer dan 40 jaar op een verantwoorde en succesvolle wijze in kansrijke Nederlandse MKB-ondernemingen met groeiambitie.\n\nMet een heldere investeringsstrategie spelen wij in op meerjarige trends in aantrekkelijke groeimarkten, waarbij wij ons focussen op Healthcare, Technology en de Agrifood tech sector.\n\n# **.**\n\nOns ervaren en betrokken investeringsteam weet wat ondernemen is en streeft naar een open, duurzame en professionele relatie met de management teams, met het gezamenlijke doel om optimale groei te realiseren.\n\n**Onze investeringsstrategie**\n\n* Focus op Healthcare, Technology & Agrifood\n* Groeifinanciering & buy-out capital\n* Actieve (hands-on) ondersteuning\n\n“Wij combineren succesvol  \nondernemerschap met ruime investeringservaring en een  \nrelevant internationaal netwerk.”\n\n![](https://hollandcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/fotorij_home_2.jpg \"fotorij_home_2\") \n\nRecente investeringen\n\n[ ](https://hollandcapital.nl/project/gullimex/ \"Gullimex\") \n\n[ ](https://hollandcapital.nl/project/blyott/ \"Blyott\") \n\n[ ](https://hollandcapital.nl/project/uman-2/ \"Uman\") \n\n[ ](https://hollandcapital.nl/project/curess-portfoliobedrijf-holland-capital/ \"Curess\") \n\n[ALLE INVESTERINGEN](https://hollandcapital.nl/portfolio/) \n\n[MAAK KENNIS MET ONS TEAM](https://hollandcapital.nl/team-3/) \n\nNieuws\n\n[](https://hollandcapital.nl/junior-office-manager/)\n\n## [ Junior Office Manager ](https://hollandcapital.nl/junior-office-manager/) \n\napr 3, 2025\n\nWij zijn op zoek naar een enthousiaste Junior Office Manager voor ons kantoor in Amsterdam. Naast de praktische ondersteuning die je onmisbaar maakt, is het vooral je persoonlijkheid en energie waarmee je dagelijks het verschil maakt op kantoor. Holland Capital is...\n\n[](https://hollandcapital.nl/inzichten-uit-het-esg-webinar-van-holland-capital-en-deloitte/)\n\n## [ Inzichten uit het ESG webinar van Holland Capital en Deloitte ](https://hollandcapital.nl/inzichten-uit-het-esg-webinar-van-holland-capital-en-deloitte/) \n\nmrt 21, 2025\n\nAfgelopen week hadden we het genoegen om, in samenwerking met Deloitte, een boeiend en inspirerend ESG-webinar te organiseren voor onze portfoliobedrijven. Tijdens de sessie verkenden we de impact van ESG door zowel de regelgeving als – nog belangrijker – de kansen voor waardecreatie te bespreken.\n\n[](https://hollandcapital.nl/gullimex-trekt-investeerder-holland-capital-aan-voor-verdere-groei/)\n\n## [ Gullimex trekt investeerder Holland Capital aan voor verdere groei ](https://hollandcapital.nl/gullimex-trekt-investeerder-holland-capital-aan-voor-verdere-groei/) \n\nmrt 10, 2025\n\nInvesteringsmaatschappij Holland Capital investeert in Gullimex, een sterke speler op het gebied van meet-, kwaliteit- en controleoplossingen in de food en medical sector. De investering van Holland Capital biedt Gullimex de mogelijkheid de gestelde groeiambities te realiseren.\n\n[](https://hollandcapital.nl/ons-portfoliobedrijf-sirius-medical-en-mammotome-gaan-samenwerking-aan-voor-distributie-van-sirius-pintuition-in-de-verenigde-staten-en-duitsland/)\n\n## [ Ons portfoliobedrijf Sirius Medical en Mammotome gaan samenwerking aan ](https://hollandcapital.nl/ons-portfoliobedrijf-sirius-medical-en-mammotome-gaan-samenwerking-aan-voor-distributie-van-sirius-pintuition-in-de-verenigde-staten-en-duitsland/) \n\nfeb 27, 2025\n\nOns portfoliobedrijf Sirius Medical, pionier op het gebied van Surgical Marker Navigation, en Mammotome, een wereldwijd erkende leider in borstkankerzorg, zijn trots om een exclusieve distributieovereenkomst voor de Verenigde Staten en Duitsland aan te kondigen.\n\n[](https://hollandcapital.nl/ons-portfolio-bedrijf-sirius-medical-haalt-groeifinanciering-op-bij-nieuwe-en-bestaande-investeerders/)\n\n## [ Sirius Medical haalt groeifinanciering op bij nieuwe en bestaande investeerders ](https://hollandcapital.nl/ons-portfolio-bedrijf-sirius-medical-haalt-groeifinanciering-op-bij-nieuwe-en-bestaande-investeerders/) \n\nfeb 4, 2025\n\nOns portfolio bedrijf Sirius Medical, een toonaangevend medisch-technologiebedrijf en marktleider in onco-chirurgische marker-navigatie, heeft een financiering van € 10 miljoen euro opgehaald op Wereldkankerdag. \n\n[](https://hollandcapital.nl/beyonder-is-de-nieuwe-naam-van-house-of-clouds/)\n\n## [ Beyonder is de nieuwe naam van House of Clouds ](https://hollandcapital.nl/beyonder-is-de-nieuwe-naam-van-house-of-clouds/) \n\njan 10, 2025\n\nHouse of Clouds heeft een belangrijke stap gezet in haar groeiambities en gaat vanaf vandaag verder onder de naam Beyonder. Tijdens een feestelijke bijeenkomst in het Eindhovense Natlab onthulde CEO Sander Dekker de nieuwe naam en merkidentiteit, samen met alle collega’s.\n\n* Solid Ventures was founded in December 2005 as the successor of the 300M. NeSBIC Converging Technologies Funds, founded in June 1997 by [Robert Wilhelm](https://www.linkedin.com/in/robertwilhelm/). \n\nVia its own strong networks built up well over 30 years with successful serial entrepreneurs and strong cooperation links and strategic partnerships with [IMPROVED Corporate Finance](https://www.improvedcf.com/) and [Drake Star Partners](https://www.drakestar.com/) and other M&A Corporate Finance Advisory firms such as [Capitalmind Investec](https://capitalmind.com/), Solid Ventures is able to source proprietary deal flow and (co-) invest in promising tech growth companies. \n\n​\n\nAlso, Solid Ventures has a strong network of local venture capitalists and respected family offices in Colombia with local strategic partnerships such as [Rockstart Colombia](https://rockstart.com/latam/) and[ Monseratte Ventures](https://www.monserrateventures.com/) in Bogota, Colombia. Through this network, Solid Ventures is able to source proprietary deal flow and (co-) invest in promising tech growth companies in this emerging market of huge opportunities bringing Latin America digitally on par with U.S. and Western - European online economies. Solid Ventures is hereby leveraging its insights and experience derived from more than 30 years venture capital tech investing in these more mature markets. \n\n​\n\nThe Partners of Solid Ventures have co-invested with a.o. i[nQlab](https://www.linkedin.com/company/inqlab/), [Tiger Capital](https://www.tigerglobal.com/), [General Atlantic](https://www.generalatlantic.com/), [Harlan Capital Partners](https://www.harlancapital.com/), [FJ Labs](https://fjlabs.com/), [Monseratte Venture](https://www.monserrateventures.com/), [C4Ventures](https://c4v.com/), [Hummingbird Ventures](https://www.hummingbird.vc/), [Volta Ventures](https://www.volta.ventures/), [Kennet Capital](https://kennet.com/), [Newion](https://www.newion.com/), [HenQ](https://henq.vc/), [DN Capital](https://www.dncapital.com/), etc.\n\nOur Focus\n\nWe focus on scale-up companies at the growth stage of development in the digital economy in general with a specific focus on the sectors: Fintech, Enterprise Software SaaS, MarketPlaces, sustainable mobility, smart energy and smart city solutions. \n\nOur Approach\n\nOur approach is building successful companies together with ambitious, experienced (serial) entrepreneurs by providing our capital, experience, network and technology and business knowledge to create internationally exitable companies at a strategic premium.\n\nOur USP's\n\nThe Unique Selling Points (USP's) of Solid Ventures compared to informal investors, family offices and other venture capitalists are:\n\n* Unmatched more than 30 years of experience proven by a track record in over 100 investments, over 50 successful strategic exits and several Initial Public Offerings (IPO's).\n* Entrepreneurial speed of professional execution in deals.\n* Strong technology and experienced business knowledge.\n* Acting as active and down-to-earth sounding board for entrepreneurs in the growth, next funding rounds and exit phases.\n* Valuable international network of co-investors for next funding rounds to expand portfolio companies rapidly.\n* Unrivaled focus on value creation by creating a clear investment exit road map together with management in 4-6 years.\n* Well connected with various tech investment banks and tech M&A advisors to secure a premium exit value for all investors involved.\n* Investment style based upon transparency, trust and respect for entrepreneurs.\n\nOur Principles \n\n* We only invest in honest entrepreneurs with reliable, professional co-investors that we can really trust!\n* We stick to our word and deliver on our promises and execute on agreements: ALWAYS!\n* We build a long term partnership with entrepreneurs and co-investors based on trust, respect, transparency and integrity!\n* Deal-by-deal tech venture capital investing at industry standard conditions.\n* High financial team commitment.\n* High moral and ethical standards (Courage, Integrity, Commitment).\n* No conflicts of interests.\n* Full transparency.\n* Co-investing with similar risk / return like minded informal investors and family offices only.\n* Investing according the [Europe Invest industry guidelines](https://www.investeurope.eu/industry-standards/)[ ](https://www.investeurope.eu/industry-standards/)only.\n* Authorized and AIFMD regulated by the Dutch Authority Financial Markets (AFM).\n\nHome: About\n\n![AdobeStock_90492285.jpeg](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/abd91f_63884724cb9e44809be1f0c095d6f6ae~mv2_d_6000_4000_s_4_2.jpeg/v1/fill/w_123,h_82,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/abd91f_63884724cb9e44809be1f0c095d6f6ae~mv2_d_6000_4000_s_4_2.jpeg)\n\n## Our Investment Criteria\n\nSolid Ventures invests in innovative and fast-growing scale up companies. We do not invest in start-ups! We focus on companies in the sectors Fintech, Enterprise Software SaaS, MarketPlaces, sustainable mobility, smart energy and smart city solutions. \n\n​\n\nWe look for companies that fit our vision, our expertise and experience. Besides, we look for the mutual click between investor and entrepreneur. Building a solid relationship is crucial in developing a company to the next level. Next to the personal aspect, we have clear investment criteria to determine our next investment. Please see our strict investment criteria below:\n\n* We only invest in honest, transparent entrepreneurs together with reliable, professional co-investors!\n* We do NOT invest in early stage start-ups, only scale-ups!\n* Minimum recurring revenues of € 1M (LATAM: € 500K) with minimum 50% annual growth.\n* An excellent and experienced management team (with serial entrepreneurs).\n* Proven internationally scale able B2B business model on 1 global platform.\n* Robust platform technology and multiple innovative products.\n* Clear value proposition and proven 'go-to-market' strategy.\n* Emerging high quality international corporate customer base.\n* Funding commitment from Solid Ventures ranging from minimum €750K (LATAM: € 500K) up to a maximum of € 5M.\n* Minority share.\n* Headquarters based in the Netherlands or Colombia (Bogota).\n\n​\n\nPlease check our investment criteria and do send us your investment proposal if there is a match ONLY\\* at [deals@solidventures.nl​](mailto:deals@solidventures.nl). \n\n\\* We do not respond to unsolicited requests for funding that do not fit our investment criteria or are sent to other mail addresses of Solid Ventures team members!\n\nHome: About Us\n\n## Our References\n\nHome: Testimonials\n\n“The Solid Ventures team acted as a very active and committed partner, even during the more difficult periods. They helped us find customers and close the first sales in the Netherlands. They have also been instrumental in critical phases to convince other investors to have confidence in the future of the company.”\n\n### Kristof de Spiegeleer\n\n### Founder & CEO DataCenterTechnologies.\n\n1. Portfolio\n\n## Our Track Record\n\n[Solid Ventures](https://www.telecompaper.com/nieuws/solid-ventures-launches-capital-fund-for-ict-start-ups--494864) has been active since December 2005 as the successor of the 300M. [NeSBIC Converging Technologies Funds](https://www.computable.nl/artikel/achtergrond/ict-branche/1328750/1444691/nesbic-haalt-120-miljoen-euro-op.html), founded in 1997\\. In 2000, this fund was one of the first and largest dedicated European tech venture funds. \n\n​\n\nOur trackrecord is built on more than 30 years of many successful investments and exits, with notable successes as KPN challengers [Versatel](https://www.buyoutsinsider.com/nesbic-fund-achieves-first-ipo-with-versatel/) (IPO NASDAQ / AEX July 1999) and [Scarlet Telecom](https://www.reuters.com/article/belgacom-scarlet-idUKWEB544220080215) (sold to Belgacom February 2008) and [Oxxio](https://www.centrica.com/media-centre/news/2005/centrica-acquires-dutch-energy-supplier/) Alternative Energy Provider acquired by Centrica (LSE:CNA) in June 2005) as challenger of the energy incumbents Eneco, Essent and Nuon. However, in the hectic early telecom and internet bubble days, we had also quite some failures such as Holland's first web retailer [HotOrange](https://www.emerce.nl/nieuws/hot-orange-vraagt-uitstel-van-betaling-aan), while we should have invested in [CoolBlue](https://www.reuters.com/business/finance/dutch-online-retailer-coolblue-postpones-ipo-due-market-conditions-2021-10-13/), European web retailer [LetsBuyIt,](http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/832597.stm)[ with an ](http://news.bbc.co.uk/2/hi/business/832597.stm)IPO on the Neuer Markt Frankfurt in July 2000 and then failed and [BaBYXL](https://www.emerce.nl/nieuws/tiscali-neemt-babyxl-over), Holland's first ADSL internet provider sold to publicly quoted [Tiscali ](https://www.wsj.com/articles/SB940201366309347922)(now [KPN Telecom](https://www.marketingfacts.nl/berichten/20060915%5Fkpn%5Fneem%5Ftiscali%5Fnederland%5Fover)) for 1 euro.... \n\nOther successful exits were ITMasters, a Belgian developer of systems management tools, acquired by [BMC Software](https://www.bizjournals.com/austin/stories/2003/03/24/daily16.html) for $42 million in cash (NYSE:BMC), DataCenterTechnologies, now PureDisk acquired by [Symantec](https://www.crn.com/news/storage/184417593/symantec-delivering-remote-office-backup-software.htm) (NASDAQ: SYMC), Dedigate (AMEX:TWW), [Immidio](https://www.eweek.com/virtualization/vmware-acquires-immidio-for-vdi-adds-bundler-for-horizon/) (now VMWare, acquired by Broadcom), [Backup Agent](https://tech.eu/2014/09/02/acronis-acquires-cloud-backup-software-backupagent/) (now Acronis).\n\n​\n\nMore than 25 years of early stage tech venture capital investing and still every day we are learning from our mistakes and enjoying our successes!\n\n[![CoolGames-logo.png](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/2b04a1_3fb0a00a9efb4d8bba3e9527cb148b7a~mv2.png/v1/fill/w_117,h_68,al_c,q_85,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_3,enc_avif,quality_auto/CoolGames-logo.png)](https://www.coolgames.com/)\n\n### [CoolGames was successfully acquired by Keesing Media Group](https://www.solidventures.vc/%5Ffiles/ugd/abd91f%5F6587fdb4c46f4f34b9574bb83ae2eba6.pdf)\n\n### [Unicorn status via follow-on funding [Runbook successfully acquired by Blackline](https://www.blackline.com/about/press-releases/2016/blackline-acquires-runbook/)\n\nHome: Portfolio\n\n## Our Team\n\nHome: Team\n\n![Foto Robert Wilhelm.jpg](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/abd91f_d94db2e64df6486f96376351e87f1488~mv2.jpg/v1/crop/x_0,y_62,w_572,h_572/fill/w_115,h_115,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/Foto%20Robert%20Wilhelm.jpg)\n\n### Robert Wilhelm\n\nFounder & Managing Partner\n\n[Robert](https://www.linkedin.com/in/robertwilhelm/) is founder of Solid Ventures. He has been active in the private equity sector for more than 30 years. He has gained experience in international venture capital and supported many early stage technology companies, both in Europe, the US and Latin America, most notably as the founder of the 300M. NeSBIC Converging Technologies Funds in the early internet days investing in B2B, B2C, software and telecom companies. He started his career at Atlas Ventures, a pioneer in the European tech venture capital scene since 1980\\. In addition to deal sourcing, he is competent and very experienced in the overall monitoring process, strategic issues and in initiating exits. He personally has raised and managed more than €400 million in fund capital. He also brings legal and corporate finance skills to the team with his experience as a tech investment banker at Drake Star Partners / IMPROVED Corporate Finance.\n\n​\n\nRobert holds an MBA from the Rotterdam School of Management and a Master Degree in Law from the Free University of Amsterdam. \n\n[LinkedIn](https://www.linkedin.com/in/robertwilhelm/)\n\n![Dennis_edited.jpg](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/abd91f_3a90705a10634f219df0b1ec14fad256~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_115,h_115,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/Dennis_edited.jpg)\n\n### Dennis Blom\n\nPartner Solid Ventures II Investments\n\n[Dennis](https://www.linkedin.com/in/deblom/) has more than 20 years of experience in technology investing. Next to that he is very experienced in guiding companies from start-up phase to the growth phase thanks to his position as Managing Partner of Silicon Polder Fund. \n\nEarly in his career he was the CTO of the first Dutch Internet Service Provider Planet Internet. \n\nDennis has been the founder of several software and video conference solutions companies, such as McNolia, Vidyo etc. \n\nDennis is an experienced board member of technology companies. \n\nHis specialties are in the field of software development, information technology and business consultancy.\n\n​\n\nDennis holds a Bachelor Degree in mechanical engineering.\n\n​\n\n​\n\nThe Partners are supported by Venture Partners, Industry Associate Partners, Analysts and Interns. \n\n​\n\n[LinkedIn](https://www.linkedin.com/in/deblom/)\n\n![fvanalkemade.jpg](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/abd91f_ad0b8643a5f9414e965dfb0905ebead2~mv2.jpg/v1/fill/w_115,h_115,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/fvanalkemade.jpg)\n\n### Floris van Alkemade\n\nCo-Founder, Managing Partner Solid Ventures I & Venture Partner Solid Ventures II Investments\n\n[Floris](https://www.linkedin.com/in/florisvanalkemade/) has co-founded Solid Ventures in 2005 with Robert Wilhelm. Floris has more than 25 years of experience in investing in seed and early stages IT and telecom companies. He has managed more than €370 million in fund capital in total. Floris has been a Partner at the NeSBIC Converging Technology Funds. In 2000 he spent time in Silicon Valley to manage the US operations for the funds. Floris is also board member at Coolgames.com, the last remaining active company in the portfolio of Solid Ventures I. \n\n​\n\nFloris holds a Master's degree in business econometrics from the Free University of Amsterdam.\n\n[LinkedIn](https://www.linkedin.com/in/florisvanalkemade/)\n\n![Foto website.webp](https://static.wixstatic.com/media/abd91f_77542589f6554b419a2c9e4f7d2afc3d~mv2.webp/v1/fill/w_106,h_115,al_c,q_80,usm_0.66_1.00_0.01,blur_2,enc_avif,quality_auto/Foto%20website.webp)\n\nCo-Investor, Associate Partner Solid Ventures II Investments\n\n[LinkedIn](https://www.linkedin.com/in/roelantvanherwaarden/)\n\n### Roelant van Herwaarden\n\nRoelant has been co-investing with Solid Ventures II since 2018 and  has been a partner at ARV Group since late 2010. number 15001346.  \n  \nDISCLAIMER   \nInvesting in early stage tech businesses involves risks, including illiquidity, lack of dividends, loss of investment and dilution. It should only be done as part of a diversified portfolio. Any co-investment opportunities are targeted exclusively at a closed group of known investors who understand the risks of investing in early stage businesses and can make their own investment decisions. Any pitches for co-investment with Solid Ventures are not to be considered as an offer to the general public, but co-investment opportunities by invitation only. The value of an Investment may go down as well as up and an Investor may not get back the full amount invested and may therefore lose some or all of their Investment. The investment opportunities offered in the Solid Ventures funds are not covered by any Financial Services Compensation Scheme.  \n  \nCONFIDENTIALITY & EXCLUSIVITY  \nSolid Ventures is registered and authorized under the AIFMD Act by the Authority Financial Markets under no. 15001346 to (co-)invest only in private companies and strictly adheres to the investment guidelines of Invest Europe. Solid Ventures only invites selected and known co-investors for its proprietary deal flow provided that this deal flow will be kept strictly confidential and for investment purposes via Solid Ventures investment vehicles only. Without prior written permission of Solid Ventures it is explicitly not allowed to share this proprietary deal flow with any other investors or approach the target, target’s management or target’s investors directly for whatever purpose, which conditions are accepted by the receipt of this information. te-files.com/661fa8ab3430151089031ec4/663212421f31780299523537_Vectors-Wrapper.svg)\n\nFounders by heart, investors by craft\n\nAt DFF, we believe in a no-nonsense approach to company building. That same philosophy drives our investment strategy. We go beyond spreadsheets and polished pitch decks, focusing on entrepreneurial grit, solid execution, and the people behind the ideas. Our founders are as relentless and resourceful as we are—a group of bold personalities who get things done. With experience building companies like WeTransfer, Just Eat, Hiber, Treatwell, and fonQ, we’ve now created the fund we wish we had back then. \"A Conversation with Jan Scholtes: Endeit’s New Venture Partner for AI\") [ All news  and blogs ![arrow white](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/arrow-white.png) ](/news) \n\n##  Why  do we do it?\n\n### In Amsterdam, our journey as a European scale\\-up investor began in 2006\\. Now, with three offices across Europe and backed by 72 entrepreneurs, we are proud of our portfolio. \n\n### **Visionary entrepreneurs**\n\nIn the canvas of innovation, the belief in the **power of technology** drives us forward. Through the landscapes of AI, machine learning, deep learning, and algorithms, we embark on a mission of **intelligent empowerment**. It’s a commitment to visionary entrepreneurs who are the architects of the future. \n\nAt our essence, we firmly believe that for scale\\-ups to thrive, **saying NO** to certain activities is key.\n\nWe’re proud to support entrepreneurs shaping the future. Our **Buy&Build strategy** effectiveness is underscored by 40 add-on acquisitions across 22 countries.\n\n### **European focus**\n\nRooted in Germany, the Netherlands, and Sweden, we catalyze change across **Europe** with our latest **€300M+ fund.** \n\nBut it’s not all about the numbers. \n\nTogether with a team of international colleagues, **we** **celebrate personal connections** **.** Entrepreneurs return for a second act; portfolio innovators join us as limited partners and former employees find their way back to contribute. \n\n### **Segments**\n\nWith AI as the overall denominator, we focus on **Future of Work, Sales Tech, Supply Chain, Fintech, AI** and **Climate Tech.**  \n  \nJoin us on a journey into the heart of **innovation**, where purposeful investment isn’t just a concept—it’s the force that shapes a brighter, more empowered future for all.\n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/uploads/2020/10/PRI.jpg)\n\n_We are a **PRI signatory** and highly value the principles for responsible investments, promoted by the United Nations._\n\nEndeit Capital really delivered WOW: super-connected and with deep domain knowledge of the digital media & adtech ecosystems, instrumental in introducing Unruly to clients and M&A targets.\n\nSarah Wood\n\nCo-founder and co-CEO Unruly,  \nUK Business Woman of the Year 2016\n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/Sarah_Wood.png?2) \n\nHaving a strategic investor like Endeit has provided benefits across a range of areas in our business, from business planning and execution through to M&A opportunities.\n\nDiane Perlman\n\nCOO Blis\n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/Diane_Perlman.png?2) \n\nWith Endeit Capital's hands-on help, we acquired four companies in 3 different continents. It has been a catalyst for the merge of Macromill and Metrixlab to create a world-class market research technology company.\n\nHan de Groot\n\nFounder Metrixlab \n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/testimonial-metrixlab.png) \n\nThe Endeit team is always helpful and supportive with their knowledge, network and expertise. Regardless which subject, from operations to fund raising to buy & build, they are our sparring partner.\n\nIngeborg Lampe\n\nCOO Roamler\n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/Ingeborg_Lampe.png?2) \n\nEndeit has been a hands-on and supportive partner to us, helping us solve our toughest business challenges.\n\nAlex Cappy\n\nCOO 3D Hubs\n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/001-Alex_Cappy.png?2) \n\nWhilst leaving room for entrepreneurial spirit, Endeit is truly supporting us with a deep understanding of the world of SaaS, enabling Virtuagym to create a healthier world.\n\nQuinten Francken-Bosman\n\nCOO Virtuagym\n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/themes/endeit/images/002-Quinten_Francken-Bosman.png?2) \n\nEver since Hubert and I founded Endeit Capital, I have very much enjoyed being involved with so many innovative and successful young entrepreneurs. \n\n**Hubert** Deitmers\n\nFounder & Managing partner\n\nHubert is the founder and Managing Partner of Endeit Capital. He served as a Supervisory Board member of numerous portfolio companies such as Virtuagym, Albumprinter, Picturae, Metrixlab, Eyeworks, and Spilgames.\n\nAs Honorary Chair of the Dutch ‘Jong Ondernemen’ Foundation, Chair of the LOEY foundation, which he co-founded, and Advisory Board Member of the Amsterdam Center of Entrepreneurship, Hubert is a prominent voice for supporting entrepreneurship. Hubert has been involved with Nyenrode New Business School since its inception and served as a board member for many years. In 2012, he also published the business book ‘Thinking BIC’.\n\nBefore founding Endeit Capital, he was an angel investor in the Dutch leading social network Hyves, where he served as Chairman of the Supervisory Board until TMG’s acquisition. Until 2005, he was a Member of the Executive Board of Endemol and played a leading role in the company’s internationalization since its IPO in 1996\\. Before Endemol, Hubert gained over eight years of international venture capital experience in Europe and the US at Atlas Venture.\n\nHe holds a Master’s Degree in Industrial Engineering and Management Science from the Eindhoven University of Technology. Together with Melissa, Hubert focuses on companies in the AI segment.\n\n[ Get in touch ](mailto:Deitmers@endeit.com \"Get in touch\")  \n[Deitmers@endeit.com](mailto:Deitmers@endeit.com \"Email adress Hubert Deitmers\") \n\n[ ](https://twitter.com/hudeit \"on Twitter\") [ ](https://www.linkedin.com/in/hubertdeitmers \"on LinkedIn\") \n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/uploads/2024/06/Sara-Resvik.jpg) \n\n**Sara** Resvik\n\nPartner\n\nSara joined Endeit Capital as a Partner in August 2024\\. Previously, she was the Managing Partner at BackingMinds VC, an early-stage fund in the Nordics.\n\nShe began her career investing for Industrifonden, a prominent Swedish investment firm. Additionally, she has experience investing for and working operationally with the Norwegian media group Schibsted and the Swedish retail group Axel Johnson, where she significantly expanded various business units.\n\nSara’s investment portfolio includes sectors such as climate tech, sales and marketing tech, energy optimization tools, proptech, and more. She has also held 12 board positions in fast-growing companies.\n\nAn alumna of Lund University, Sara holds a Master of Science in Technology Management and a Bachelor in Business and Economics.\n\nBased in Stockholm, Sweden, she will lead Endeit’s Nordic investments and together with Emmelie, she focusses on companies in the Climate Tech segment.\n\n[ Get in touch ](mailto:Sara@endeit.com \"Get in touch\")  \n[Sara@endeit.com](mailto:Sara@endeit.com \"Email adress Sara Resvik\") \n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/uploads/2015/10/endeit_060422-177p.jpg) \n\n**Martijn** Hamann\n\nPartner\n\nMartijn is a Co-owner of Endeit Capital and joined Endeit Capital at the start as a Partner in 2006\\. He is focused on deals in DACH.\n\nFrom 2003 – 2006 he was a member of the Executive Director team of Endemol Group, the world’s largest independent provider of multi-screen content. He joined Endemol in 1996\\. As Executive Director he was responsible for International Operations, managing the worldwide key subsidiaries, as well as developing new business and new markets. Prior he was heading the global M&A activities at Endemol. Until 1996, Martijn was consultant at the leading Dutch M&A boutique Reitsma & Wertheim (Investec).\n\nHe holds a BA in Economics and MSc Business Administration from the Erasmus University – Rotterdam School of Management – Rotterdam, The Netherlands.\n\nHe is currently a Board member at portfolio companies Sharpist (DE, coaching platform), LePaya (NL, education tech), Happen and Infraspeak (PT). Martijn was previously on the Board at (exited) portfolio companies Blis (UK, location-powered advertising & analytics platform), Chronext (CH/DE, new & pre-owned luxury watches platform), Gastrofix (DE), Contorion (DE), Gridscale (DE), Unruly (UK), Smartclip (DE), Improve Digital (NL), Spil Games (NL), Advance (NL), CBV (PT) and Accepte/Paylogic (NL).\n\nMartijn, together with Niclas, mainly focuses on companies within the Future of Work segment together with Niclas and Sophie.\n\n[ Get in touch ](mailto:martijn@endeit.com \"Get in touch\")  \n[martijn@endeit.com](mailto:martijn@endeit.com \"Email adress Martijn Hamann\") \n\n[ ](https://twitter.com/martijnha \"on Twitter\") [ ](https://www.linkedin.com/in/martijnha \"on LinkedIn\") \n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/uploads/2022/05/endeit_060422-044_editp.jpg) \n\n**Emmelie** Meurs\n\nAssociate\n\nEmmelie joined as Business Analyst after finishing her internship at Endeit and is based in Amsterdam. He founded his first HR-Tech Start-Up in 1999 (SQUEAKER – Exit to F.A.Z.). He has founded the largest Future of Work Tech angel network in the DACH region (HR Angel Club) in 2023 and has since invested in over 10 pre-seed rounds in this space.\n\nHe has worked as a venture capitalist in London, as a strategy consultant with Oliver Wyman in Munich and as an Interim Managing Director at XING. He holds a Master in Business Management and international management from University of Cologne. Stefan is a member of YPO.\n\nStefan lives in Berlin with his wife and two kids and enjoys cooking for family and friends whenever he can.\n\n[ Get in touch ](mailto:Stefan@endeit.com \"Get in touch\")  \n[Stefan@endeit.com](mailto:Stefan@endeit.com \"Email adress Stefan Menden\") \n\n![](https://endeit.com/assets/uploads/2023/09/IMG_1041.jpg) \n\n**Tamara** Hartman\n\nContent Marketer \n\nTamara Hartman joined Endeit Capital in 2023 as a part-time Content Marketer and Social Media Manager. solutions across Europe, Middle East, Southeast Asia and the Pacific. With a unified API, the company enables mid-market merchants, ISOs, ISVs, and platforms to efficiently manage pay-in and pay-out operations across multiple geographies. By offering locally licensed acquiring and multi-currency settlement services, Nomupay simplifies cross-border payments and improves conversion rates. Headquartered in Dublin, the company employs c. 200 people across several offices globally.\n\n[nomupay.com](https://nomupay.com \"Visit the Nomupay website\") \n\nInfraspeak\n\n2024\n\nInfraspeak is an Intelligent Maintenance Management Platform, trusted by over 60,000 front-line technicians worldwide working on over 240,000 buildings. Lepaya’s curriculum centres around the idea of developing ‘power skills’ (i.e. resilience) across 60 modules (“hiring for success, presenting with confidence, or fostering diversity and inclusion”), with the focus on practical application so the skill is deeply embedded.\n\n[www.lepaya.com](https://www.lepaya.com \"Visit the Lepaya website\") \n\nSastrify\n\n2023\n\nSastrify is the leading European digital procurement platform for Software-as-a-Service (SaaS) products, helping companies to manage and reduce cost of their existing SaaS stack, as well as purchase additional 3rd party SaaS solutions via Sastrify’s marketplace.\n\nFounded by Sven Lackinger and Maximilian Messing in 2020, Sastrify’s platform automatically monitors cost, usage, GDPR compliance, renewals and other related parameters, helping companies to improve the overall software negotiation process.\n\n[www.sastrify.com](https://www.sastrify.com \"Visit the Sastrify website\") \n\nIPRally\n\n2023\n\nThe IPRally team have built a Patent Search engine and Patent classifier driven by their proprietary Graph AI technology. various initiatives to encourage entrepreneurship\n\nBased on our ‘**Thinking BIC**’ philosophy (Believe, Innovate & Internationalize, Collaborate), we stimulate entrepreneurship in numerous ways and keep our entrepreneurs together with **Endeit Fellows.**\n\nKey supporting activities we co-founded are **LOEY Foundation** (Leading Online Entrepreneur of the Year; co-founded in 2010), **Venturepreneurs’ Organisation** (serial German entrepreneurs being angel investors; co-founded in 2010), and **VEECEE** (Young VC professionals; co-founded in 2015).\n\nWe are also one of the two Founding Partners of **ai.nl** (making impact-disrupting technologies comprehensible).\n\nBesides, we are involved in **various other activities** such as Jong Ondernemen (Young Entrepreneurship groundbreaking visions for a regenerative and sustainable future.\n\n[ Get started ](https://rockstart1.typeform.com/to/qoieotFj)\n\n###  Build on a solid foundation \n\n We are here to empower you along your founder journey, through investment from start to series B. We show you how to plan and strategize the next steps for your business, preparing you for fundraising and introducing you to the right co-investors.\n\n###  Streamline your vision \n\n We won’t waste your time with lecture-style presentations, but we will focus on matching you with relevant experts and mentors to support you with your most important challenges.\n\n###  Get relevant connections \n\n The success of your founder journey lies with you, but joining our global community of ambitious founders will get you on the radar of top investors and industry players, helping drive exposure for your startup at the right time and place.\n\n## Founder success stories\n\nOur portfolio companies have made exceptional achievements both financially and in terms of positive impact.\n\n\"When joining Rockstart what we really needed was structure and guidance on how on earth you start a startup. Then a network: we met our first investors at Rockstart. In fact our lead investment for our first round was our mentor.\"\n\n**Simon Bushell** – CEO and Founder, Sympower\n\nSympower secured €22M to accelerate Europe's energy transition\n\n\"It was great to have Rockstart as an investor, we also stayed part of the community for several years, that meant we could continue to access the Rockstart experience and the mentors for the first three years.\"\n\n**Bram de Zwart & Brian Garret**  – Co-founders, HUBS\n\nAcquired by Protolabs in January 2021 for $280M\n\n\"Rockstart has been and remains to be very helpful in fundraising. Their wide network in energy venturing has helped us find the right investors and ensured setting up a deal structure that was right for everyone.\"\n\n**Hubert Penn** – CCO, Dexter\n\nRaised a €2M Series A round to accelerate the energy transition\n\n“Being part of Rockstart was a gaming-changing moment for iClinic and the first inflexion point in our history. It provided us for the first time the ways to achieve our big vision and showed how far we would be able to go.”\n\n**Felipe Lourenço** – CEO, iClinic\n\nAcquired by Afya Limited for €27.9M in 2020\n\n\"Rockstart helped in taking our company from an idea to raising €3M+ in less than 12 months. They taught us what it means to run a business, raise capital, and build a strategy. They are still the ones we call when we have challenges or need to make important decisions.\"\n\n**Emil Munck de Voss** – Co-founder, REDUCED\n\nSecured €8M in 2024 to scale natural food ingredients business\n\n\"Agtech is one of the biggest upcoming investment possibilities, and Rockstart understands the sphere, and also how to move and become successful in the area. This is why we picked Rockstart.\"\n\n**John Smedegaard** – Co-founder & CEO\n\nLanded €3M from Danish Agro and the Pajbjerg Foundation in late 2024.\n\n## We are Rockstart\n\nWith a global network and offices in Amsterdam, Copenhagen and Bogotá, we’re on a mission to empower founders to drive positive change on a global scale. We know from experience that most early-stage founders face challenges in several key areas when growing their startups. Our team of commercially seasoned entrepreneurs guides you on how to optimize your time and resources to achieve the highest possible output. \n\nWe provide proven fast-track scaling solutions for purpose-driven founders operating in Energy, AgriFood and Emerging Technology – through domain-focused, tailor-made, mentor-driven support packages, market introductions and investments from pre-seed to series B.\n\n[ AgriFood ](https://rockstart.com/agrifood/)\n\n[ Energy ](https://rockstart.com/energy/)\n\n[ Emerging Tech ](https://rockstart.com/emerging-tech/)\n\n350+\n\nStartups invested in\n\n$1.7bn\n\nAlumni value\n\n€360m+\n\nRaised by startups\n\n## Our Global Ecosystem\n\nWe believe that the fastest route to a sustainable future is by building partnerships that last, and our global community of mentors, investors and corporate partners is the driving force behind everything we do. We’ve built a diverse ecosystem of professionals around the globe, providing founders with industry-specific expertise and a launching pad to take solutions directly to the market.\n\nOur corporate programs have allowed our founders to work with some of the world’s leading companies, resulting in faster routes to commercial partnerships and investment. Some of our notable corporate initiatives include [Ørsted Propel](https://propel.orsted.com/), [Amsterdam Circular](https://www.ams-institute.org/entrepreneurship/amsterdam-circular/), or the Dutch Entrepreneurial Development Bank’s (FMO) Finture Solutions.\n\n## Are you interested in joining us  \nas a corporate partner?\n\nWe work with companies who want to join our mission to drive faster Capital](/over-craft-capital) \n\nPause\n\n# Wat kan Craft Capital voor jou betekenen?\n\nCraft Capital investeert in meerderheidsbelangen in Nederlandse bedrijven met een EBITDA vanaf EUR 2 miljoen. Samen met de ondernemer creëren we meerwaarde via organische groei, expansie in nieuwe markten en/of via een buy-and-build-strategie.\n\n[ Meer over onze werkwijze ](/werkwijze) \n\n## Hier staan wij voor\n\n* Ondernemerschap  \n Als ervaren ondernemers en professionals weten we wat de succesfactoren zijn voor verdere groei\n* Gezamenlijkheid  \n Craft Capital werkt nauw samen met de ondernemer en het management team om het bedrijf naar een volgend niveau te brengen\n* Eerlijkheid  \n Craft Capital doet op een oprechte manier zaken. We zijn transparant en zuiver, daar kun je ons ook op afrekenen\n\n## Ontmoet ons team\n\n Nuchter, no-nonsense en betrokken. Something went wrong while submitting the form.\n\n[Learn More](/prexlr-lp)\n\n# We help build\n\n# commercially successful innovations\n\nAchieving success in the competitive field of innovation hinges not just on taking the right steps, but also on doing them in the correct order.\n\nProperly timing the critical activities can be the key difference between a prospering and a faltering intrapreneur. We help our clients hit that timing just right to let them succeed.\n\n![Modern architecture roof Tilburg central station\n](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/64525768e6ab513a4679e933_DSC_7994A%20regular%20small%20(1).webp)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425e4c575b7752383f5c_square%20white.svg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425caa6053131572c4b5_bl.svg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425d79fb9d6897183898_square%20blue.svg)\n\nThat’s where we come in\n\n## We commercially accelerate innovation through validation\n\nWe breed blue whales\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/6790bd091b59c86948d5afca__DSC6263zw(2).jpg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425d79fb9d6897183898_square%20blue.svg)\n\nWe are in the business of testing and confirming whether a product, service or business idea addresses and fulfills the needs, wants or pain points of its intended users or customers. Proper validation is crucial for determining if a business model can thrive in the actual market. This process is the foundational step towards cultivating \"blue whales\" — businesses that are not only large but also sustainable and capable of consistent growth.\n\n200+\n\nProjects helped\n\n20.000.000\n\nSaved in bad investments\n\n## Does this mean that we work on this with you?\n\nYes. We are invested in innovation, excited about the process and like-minded when it comes to entrepreneurship.\n\n[![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425c767e05226c315fd2_circle%20black.svg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425dcdeb8c4159bb5d90_circle%20text.svg)![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425c62816161c0e1aa9a_circle%20arrow.svg)](/discovery-call)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c65eb3c0d45481d9b0c80_Rectangle%2021.svg)\n\nInnovation can sprout from idealism, but it can also be enforced by the need for growth. Either way, innovation is a process of ongoing iteration, fickle and it is generally hard to predict.\n\nDo we want to mitigate risk by putting together a sustainable innovation portfolio? Absolutely. But we especially want to be realistic about success.\n\nWe make sure that your idea meets the market in a way that is relevant for your end user, whether that is a consumer or a business. That also means that if it isn’t considered relevant, we advise against going ahead with the idea.\n\n![innogy](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c422a6a4a36f56c8835b0_image%2012-min.png)\n\n![kpn](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c422ac3279a431394aeb0_image%2014-min.png)\n\n![Logo innovations we provide the following services.\n\n01 // \n\n## Innovation Strategy\n\n[We assist you in crafting an innovation strategy tailored to your organization's specific needs, innovation style, and operational flexibility.![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425cb8d59640b54a2620_arrow%20on%20blue.svg)Innovation Stategy - ](/services/innovation-strategy)\n\n02 //\n\n## PreXLR\n\n[A focused 12-week program, led by an experienced facilitator, designed to assess the commercial potential of an idea by systematically validating or eliminating uncertainties and risks. The end result is not just a validated plan, but committed customers.![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425cb8d59640b54a2620_arrow%20on%20blue.svg)PreXLR - ](/services/prexlr)\n\n03 //\n\n## Go-to-Market\n\n[After PreXLR (or having a properly validated idea), embark on a 6-month journey through which we help you focus on four critical areas: Sales & Marketing, Products, Operations, and Team. This program is designed to build the foundation for a scalable and robust business, setting the stage for enduring success. ![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/632c352ebcded80cb8b630c1/632c425cb8d59640b54a2620_arrow%20on%20blue.svg)Go-to-Market - ](/services/go-to-market)\n\n04 //\n\n## Senior Validator\n\n[Validators are experts of momentum, serving as efficient additions to your teams that ensure progress. They play a key role in conducting experiments, identifying subsequent steps, and are experienced in our methodology. Buying ESG shares only help shareholders, it does not fund the underlying companies to scale their technologies, whereas investing with Carbon Equity does.\n\n![Person who wrote the testimonial](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/62eb8ccb51692698f4ded799/657c2ce5d0992315ace57a2d_Photo%20(2).webp)\n\nMadelein Smit\n\nCOO, Sendcloud\n\nMaintaining our wealth by developing innovative sustainable solutions is the best hope we have — and that's exactly what Carbon Equity does. It allows more individuals to play a pivotal role in accelerating climate tech companies.\n\n![Person who wrote the testimonial](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/62eb8ccb51692698f4ded799/657c2ced76b4621be4c764fc_Photo-1.webp)\n\nFrans Haafkens\n\nFounding Partner, i4hi\n\nFrictionless investing\n\n## Pick your investment strategy\n\n### Select your investment focus\n\nYou choose between a diversified set of funds or one fund focused on the companies that matter most to you.\n\n![next](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/62eb8ccb51692698f4ded799/631630b33bdc3f050d0fb3e2_next-in-process.svg)\n\n### Investments are aggregated\n\nYour capital is bundled with other investors to let you reach the requirements of investing with first-class investment teams.\n\n![next](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/62eb8ccb51692698f4ded799/631630b33bdc3f050d0fb3e2_next-in-process.svg)\n\n### The climate journey begins\n\nYour investment team invests for you so Neither Carbon Equity B.V. nor the funds it manages are subject to regulatory supervision by any other regulatory authority than the Dutch Authority for the Financial Markets.\n\nCarbon Equity B.V. does not offer investment advice. Investments into private equity are speculative and risky. The value of investments can vary over time. Investments into private equity have a long horizon (exceeding 10 years) with **no or** limited liquidity. If you cannot afford to potentially lose your full investment, it is best not to invest. Past performance does not guarantee future returns. Partners voor echte waardecreatie\n\nBolster Investment Partners is een flexibele, lange termijn investeerder. Wij zijn gespecialiseerd in samenwerkingen met DGA- en familiebedrijven middels minderheids- en meerderheidsbelangen. Bolster investeert in buitengewone Nederlandse ondernemingen met een scherpe focus en een bewezen business model. Bolster ondersteunt ondernemers bij het realiseren van het volledige potentieel van hun onderneming. Door als gelijkwaardige partners het verschil te maken.\n\n[Meer over ons](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/over-ons/) \n\n[ Huidige investeringen Leeuwendaal **Feiten** ''Sinds 1999 ontdekten 30 miljoen mensen hun talenten met CliftonStrengths, in Nederland exclusief aangeboden door Leeuwendaal'' ](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/investeringen/leeuwendaal/) [ Huidige investeringen WIND Subsea Cable Services **Feiten** \"WIND heeft al meer dan 100.000km buiten gebruik gestelde onderzeese kabels verwijderd en gerecycled\" ](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/investeringen/wind-subsea-cable-services/) [ Huidige investeringen Kwabo **Feiten** \"Per jaar produceert Kwabo ruim 2,5 keer de omtrek van de aarde aan afdekmateriaal uit gerecyclede grondstoffen\" ](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/investeringen/kwabo/) [ Huidige investeringen SelektHuis **Feiten** \"SelektHuis heeft in 42 jaar ruim 8.000 unieke vrijstaande woningen gebouwd vanuit een gestandaardiseerd flexibel bouwsysteem\" ](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/investeringen/selekthuis/) [ Huidige investeringen Snoeks Automotive **Feiten** \"Jaarlijks worden meer dan 80.000 bedrijfswagens uitgerust met interieurconcepten van Snoeks\" ](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/investeringen/snoeks-automotive/) [ Huidige investeringen BTG Positioning Systems **Feiten** \"De producten van BTG worden wereldwijd ingezet in ca. 100 container havens, verdeeld over 38 landen.\" ](https://bolsterinvestments.nl/investeringen/btg-positioning-systems/) [ Huidige investeringen Dinnissen Cooll](/projects/cooll/)\n\n###### [Financial Advisory for Knitwear Lab](/projects/knitwear-lab/)\n\n###### [Investment in Momo Medical](/projects/momo-medical/)\n\n###### [M&A Advisory for investors we understand the development and funding roadmap by personal experience. We strive to be a sparring partner throughout the clients' growth trajectory and towards and beyond exit.\n\n## Services\n\n##### M&A Advisory\n\nWe advise on mergers and acquisitions, joint ventures, partnerships and exits, for both buyers and sellers.\n\n[](/services/ma-advisory/) \n\n##### Financial Advisory\n\nWe assists clients with fundraising, valuation, due diligence, financial modeling, deal structuring and negotiation, for both equity and debt transactions.\n\n[](/services/financial-advisory/) \n\n##### Strategic Advisory\n\nWe help clients with market research, business planning, strategy formulation, impact assessment, stakeholder engagement and communication.\n\n[](/services/strategic-advisory) \n\n##### Investments\n\nWe pool investments from private investors to allow them to participate in deal-by-deal investments which are normally only possible with larger tickets.\n\n[](/services/our-own-investments) \n\n###### Our story\n\n## About No Five Trees\n\nNo Five Trees’ founders have a long track record in financing, financial and general management and supporting investments with a wide range of services. We started No Five Trees because on the one hand we experienced an opportunity to provide structuring, financing or management advise to parties that could definitely use it, but in most cases cannot afford it yet. On the other hand we see a lot of parties and people with both the willingness and financial means to invest together with us.\n\n[More about us](/about/)\n\n###### Are we a good fit?\n\n## Our clients are:\n\n![thumbnail no five trees wit](https://nofivetrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/NFT-thumbnail-wit.svg) \n\n#### Startups\n\nWe empower startups with comprehensive support in market research, financial planning, fundraising, and strategic growth initiatives.\n\n![thumbnail no five trees wit](https://nofivetrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/NFT-thumbnail-wit.svg) \n\n#### Small enterprises\n\nWe enable small enterprises to thrive by offering expert guidance in business case development, financial strategy, and investment solutions tailored to their needs.\n\n![thumbnail no five trees wit](https://nofivetrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/NFT-thumbnail-wit.svg) \n\n#### Medium-sized enterprises\n\nWe support medium-sized enterprises with strategic advice and investment expertise to optimise operations, foster growth, and achieve long-term sustainability.\n\n###### Our strong points\n\n## Why No Five Trees\n\n##### **Investment & Advise**\n\nWe can offer a combination of investment and advisory services to your organisation, ensuring that our interests are aligned.\n\n##### **Large network**\n\nWe bring a network of investors and experts to the table for a short or longer period of time to support your company.\n\n##### **Tailor made solutions**\n\nWe provide solutions that fit the needs and goals of each client, leveraging our network of partners and advisors across sectors and regions.\n\n##### **End-to-end support**\n\nWe provide end-to-end support, from ideation and validation, to fundraising and deal-making, to execution and monitoring, to scaling and exit.\n\n##### **Relationship is key**\n\nOf course, we are focused on the deal, but we also create longstanding relationships between all parties. We believe that enduring partnerships lead to sustained success and mutual growth.\n\n##### **Honest & Realistic**\n\nWe are honest to our clients and participants, highlighting areas for improvement constructively while appreciating the positives.\n\n##### **Collaboration & Innovation**\n\nWe work together with entrepreneurs and investors, who share our common vision of creating positive change through collaboration and innovation.\n\n## Projects & Clients we're proud of\n\n#### Filter\n\n[All](#)[Financial Advisory](#)[Investment](#)[M&A Advisory](#)[Strategic Advisory](#)\n\n[](https://nofivetrees.com/projects/vt-group/)[Financial Advisory](https://nofivetrees.com/project-type/financial-advisory/)[M&A Advisory](https://nofivetrees.com/project-type/ma-advisory/)\n\n### [VT Group](https://nofivetrees.com/projects/vt-group/)\n\n[](https://nofivetrees.com/projects/cooll/)[Financial Advisory](https://nofivetrees.com/project-type/financial-advisory/)[Investment](https://nofivetrees.com/project-type/investment/)[Strategic Advisory](https://nofivetrees.com/project-type/strategic-advisory/)\n\n### [Cooll](https://nofivetrees.com/projects/cooll/)\n\n[](https://nofivetrees.com/projects/certscanner/)[Financial Advisory](https://nofivetrees.com/project-type/financial-advisory/)\n\n### [CertScanner](https://nofivetrees.com/projects/certscanner/)\n\n[See all Projects](/projects/)\n\n![](https://nofivetrees.com/wp-content/uploads/2024/05/thumbmail.png) \n\n###### Get in touch\n\n## Want to know more about what we do?\n\nWant to know more about what No Five Trees can do for you?
