we do\n\nWe invest in specialized sectors, partnering with teams ready to scale internationally.\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642443937d66db1d2617f7fb/64246ceefebfcf5ed4acebe5_Recycle-1.png)\n\n### Sustainability and Impact\n\nWe focus on businesses that leverage technology for positive change while adapting sustainable practices.\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642443937d66db1d2617f7fb/64257b302004e8168eb0f216_Vectors-Wrapper.svg)\n\n### Early to mid-stage growth companies\n\nWe look for capital efficient, scalable companies with proven product-market fit and a defensible business model.\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642443937d66db1d2617f7fb/64246cef77942b1551bc93be_Vectors-Wrapper.svg)\n\n### Proven technology\n\nWe select scalable and protected technology as proven by a reputable customer base.\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/642443937d66db1d2617f7fb/64246cf0dfe370edd5669be4_Vectors-Wrapper.svg)\n\n### Focus on Europe\n\nWe operate in an underserved but attractive market like European tech.\n\n[Learn more](/about)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/6489cd2fe7b2fd62358eecd3_gordon-willoughby-2021-by-the-canals.jpeg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/647624c735e342c5a62ffb75_WeTransfer%20original%20white.png)\n\n## HPE Growth presents itself as an investor that has ESG firmly embedded in its DNA. Given WeTransfer’s B Corp status, their collaborative approach makes them a very supportive partner with a focus on key value drivers and adding value when they know that they can. HPE was helpful in developing the subscription revenue side of WeTransfer’s business. They provided a clear roadmap on how to grow this aspect of the company and leveraged their sector expertise of best practices for growing SaaS companies. \n\n### Gordon Willoughby\n\nFormer CEO\n\n[Read their story](/portfolio-companies/wetransfer)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/64b144c74c4945237a215b52_Uberall-Founders-David-Federhen-Florian-Huebner.jpg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/647627265ae9979ceb63853b_Uberall_Logo_White.png)\n\n## We have developed a great deal of trust in our partnership with HPE. We know that their ongoing support plays a big role in building out our cutting-edge location marketing platform to connect local businesses with their customers, bridging online and offline.\n\n# Florian Hübner\n\nFounder and Co-CEO at Uberall\n\n[Read their story](/portfolio-companies/uberall)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/6489cd96051ca65d072cca77_Simon-Black_CEO-ppro.jpg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/64762710f8c05df85d3e42ea_ppro_logo_white.png)\n\n## HPE Growth is very supporting and capable of bringing both strategic and financial players into the fold. Their strong shared culture with individuals who are humble, open and very straightforward has allowed for a seamless and trusted partnership with PPRO. When it comes to investment solutions, HPE has demonstrated great creativity and execution, providing guidance in helping us structure deals and navigate this process. \n\n# Simon Black\n\nCEO\n\n[Read their story](/portfolio-companies/ppro)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/6489cc4258bbd93d48bdebe4_Malte%20Dummel_XEMPUS_COO%26CFO-2023.jpg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/647627ec2ddd074fcd6c809b_XEMPUS-white-logo.png)\n\n## HPE Growth has a balanced and structured approach towards value creation. Whenever Xempus faced a potential area for growth, we could always rely on HPE’s wider network. Their strong reputation and speed with which they understood the markets and business models with which Xempus operates made them stand at the forefront of other investors. Xempus “wouldn’t be anywhere near” where they are today without HPE’s continued support. \n\n# Malte Dummel\n\nCOO & CFO\n\n[Read their story](/portfolio-companies/xempus)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/6489d046f5053db0b312b0ee_Philipp.Roesch.Schlanderer%20copy.jpg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/64425107f35afa8972d799d3_EGYM_logo_white_color_RGB.png)\n\n## “With HPE, I have found true partners and supporters on our mission. I find working together fantastic because, I not only get the deal team if I need them, but the entire firm. Everyone’s style is to support me as an entrepreneur on my personal journey as well as creating a unique and highly impactful business.\n\n# Philip Roesch-Schlanderer\n\nCEO at EGYM\n\n[Read their story](/portfolio-companies/egym)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/64424998a270351ecb734dae_Tiqets%20-%20Testimonials.jpg)\n\n![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/643e82c8bb92ba6cf1f7bbe8/644251326d2dc42074a01243_204170-tiqets-logotype-color-320-426944-original-1460638766.png)\n\n## HPE promised more than only funds to grow. And they delivered. They actively supported me, the team and the business to grow faster, hire better people and make fewer mistakes. \n\n# Luuc Elzinga\n\nFounder of Tiqets\n\n[Read their story](/portfolio-companies/tiqets)\n\nOur impact\n\n## An investment platform where purpose and growth meet\n\nWe are on a mission to build world-class technology and purpose-driven growth organizations. The round \\[...\\] \n\n[ read more ](https://conventcapital.nl/en/convent-capital-participates-in-tidal-visions-140m-series-b-round-to-scale-chitosan-technologies-globally/) \n\n# **About Convent Capital**\n\nConvent Capital is an independent Dutch investment company established in 2011\\. With our first fund we focus on small to medium sized companies within the Benelux that have a good track record and where we see strategic and operational opportunities to create sustainable value: organically, in new markets or via a buy-&-build strategy. With our new fund we focus on providing growth capital to innovative and sustainable companies in the agri & food markets and thereby making a positive impact.\n\nConvent Capital has a strong focus on sustainability and believes in the transition from the current linear economy to a circular economy. Convent’s ambition is to prove that companies that focus on this will ultimately be the winners of the future. We are convinced that this will create higher returns for all our stakeholders in the long term. Our focus is therefore on the long term.\n\nWe do this with a team of ambitious specialists in cooperation with the management teams of our portfolio companies, supported by our investors who are all entrepreneurs of good repute and form a solid basis from which we can invest.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2016/02/Respo1.jpg) \n\n## Strategy\n\nConvent Capital’s first fund focuses on investments at the lower end of the Dutch SME market, on companies in existing sectors with strong positions and attractive growth prospects. The companies in which we participate usually have a profitability (EBITDA) between EUR 2 and 8 million. Participations arise from management buy-ins or buy-outs, spin-offs or succession issues of entrepreneurs. In this segment we always strive for a majority shareholding, whereby we always encourage the continuing management to co-invest alongside us in order to achieve an extra strong partnership between the managers and shareholders. We actively support our participations in seizing the opportunities of the Circular Economy.\n\nWith its second fund, Convent focuses on innovative companies in the Agri & Food sector that are looking for growth capital. We invest in companies that are sustainable at heart and contribute with their products and services to a healthier and sustainable food & agri value chain. Given the international and globally integrated food production markets, with this fund we invest internationally in companies throughout the OECD markets. We can invest up to EUR 15m in total per company. We like to work together with other investors to form strong consortia to be able to support our investments in the long term. And together with the entrepreneurs that run the companies day-to-day, we strive to increase their positive impact going forward.\n\n## Portfolio Agri Food Growth Fund\n\n[![Animal Health Team\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08566-scaled-e1718961816146.jpg) \n\n#### Maarten Meijnen  \n Founding Partner \n\nMaarten has been working as an investor for some time. Before he founded Convent Capital in 2011, he worked at Egeria for five years. Maarten started his professional career in 2004 at Rabobank, where he worked in the leveraged finance department. At both Rabobank and Egeria he did numerous transactions from a financing and equity perspective, both nationally and internationally.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08584-scaled-e1718961861356.jpg) \n\n#### Dirk Hoorn  \n Founding Partner \n\nPrior to founding Convent Capital, Dirk worked for two years at Royal Vopak N.V. Here he was responsible for international M&A transactions in Asia, Latin America and Europe. Dirk started his professional career in 2004 at Loyens & Loeff N.V. as a corporate lawyer specializing in M&A / private equity transactions.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/07/Steven-1-scaled-e1721303370766.jpg) \n\n#### Steven Bernaert  \n Principal \n\nSteven has been working at Convent Capital since the summer of 2014\\. He started his career as a strategy consultant at Spring Associates, mainly in the areas of sustainability, renewable energy and financial services. Steven has a master’s degree in Econometrics & Operations Research from the University of Amsterdam.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08491-scaled-e1718961755951.jpg) \n\n#### Adriaan Vrij  \n Principal \n\nAdriaan started at Convent in September 2017. Before this, he worked for 6 years as a strategy consultant at Bain & Company. There he focused on growth strategies, transformations and integrations and was involved in advisory processes for PE funds. Adriaan has studied medicine and psychology at the University of Groningen and Harvard.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08526-scaled-e1718962515181.jpg) \n\n#### Ingrid Mulder  \n CFO \n\nIngrid joined Convent Capital in May 2024 as CFO. She has 20 years’ experience in (executive) finance roles in investment banking and financial services combined with a strong operational, governance and risk background.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08510-scaled-e1718961290771.jpg) \n\n#### Bor Boer  \n Principal \n\nBor started his career with Rabobank’s Corporate Bank and Finance departments in Asia and Europe, predominately focused large Food and Agriculture clients. Hereafter Bor co-founded TerraProtein Equity Partners, a corporate finance boutique focussing on Agrifood and Agtech companies. Bor currently sits on the board of the Coexa S.A. and is a mentor in Rockstart’s Agrifood program.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/10/DSC09381-scaled-e1729601852359.jpg) \n\n#### Reynier Arendsen de Wolff  \n Principal \n\nReynier began his career as tax lawyer at NautaDutilh, after which he joined Royal Vopak (LATAM) focusing on BD and M&A projects. Here he worked together with Dirk on the acquisition of Vopak’s first LNG terminal in Mexico. Before joining Convent he worked as independent CF advisor (M&A and fund raising) and gained operational experience in cattle farming and forestation businesses.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08536-scaled-e1718961903613.jpg) \n\n#### Stephen McLoughlin  \n Operational Director \n\nStephen started in operational roles within agricultural companies within Southern Africa focusing on sustainable and socially responsible farming practises. After moving to the UK in 2012, he did an MBA and went on to co-found TerraProtein Equity Partners, focussing on raising growth capital for numerous Agrifood and Agtech companies.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08387-scaled-e1718962630340.jpg) \n\n#### Sanne Bootsma  \n Associate \n\nSanne started her career at Kempen Capital Management where she focused on responsible investing. Afterwards Sanne worked for 3 years at Transaction Services within the M&A department of Deloitte, where she was involved in the development of the sustainability due diligence proposition in addition to financial due diligence work. Sanne holds a masters in Finance from the Vrije Universiteit of Amsterdam.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08609-scaled-e1718961989558.jpg) \n\n#### Roel van der Molen  \n Investment Manager \n\nRoel, investment manager since 2023, has gained experience in strategy development & execution at Roland Berger. Here he supported companies with growth, investment and sustainability issues. He laid his financial foundation in Rotterdam with studies in both Finance and Law.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08393-scaled-e1718961951293.jpg) \n\n#### Flo Schepers  \n Associate \n\nFlo started her career at Startgreen Capital, an impact investor focused on renewables, circular economy and diversity. Before, she interned at Goodwell Investments, an investor in emerging markets. She holds an Int. Business degree from the University of Groningen and a Msc in Entrepreneurship from the University of Amsterdam.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08467-scaled-e1718961378728.jpg) \n\n#### Sabine Brans  \n Office Manager \n\nSabine started in July 2023 at Convent Capital as an office manager. She has extensive experience in office management, project management and marketing support in the healthcare sector. Sabine is hands-on and gets energy from arranging everything down to the last detail.\n\n![](https://conventcapital.nl/wp-content/uploads/2024/06/DSC08503-scaled-e1718962033524.jpg) \n\n#### Tijmen Nanninga  \n Investment Manager \n\nPrior to joining Convent Capital in 2024, Tijmen worked in the M&A team of J.P. Morgan, advising a range of clients across Europe with a focus on the mid-market. Tijmen started his career at ABN AMRO, where he joined the corporate banking traineeship in the Global Sectors department. Investment Fund background 1](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/background-1.svg) \n\n![Dutch Student Investment Fund background 1](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/background.svg) \n\n## We provide funding for innovative student startups\n\nIf you are a student of the University of Twente or Saxion and plan on building your company in Overijssel, Dutch Student Investment Fund is your launching pad.\n\n[ Apply for funding ](https://www.dsif.nl/apply-for-funding/) \n\n![Dutch Student Investment Fund background 1](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/background-1.svg) \n\n![Dutch Student Investment Fund background 1](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2018/10/background.svg) \n\n## Investment fund for students, by students!\n\nDutch Student Investment Fund (DSIF) is a venture capital fund managed by students from the University of Twente and Saxion University of Applied Sciences. It was established in 2016 as the first student-run European venture capital fund. DSIF invests up to €10.000 into innovative start-ups created by bachelor and master students, PhDs and recent graduates. The fund aims to help young student entrepreneurs to turn their great ideas into real start-ups.\n\nWhile DSIF is structured as a venture capital fund, its primary goal is not to make the biggest return on investment but rather to support student entrepreneurs as much as possible. DSIF believes that young entrepreneurs should have access to all the means necessary to turn their great ideas into real start-ups that could potentially benefit society.\n\n### Mission\n\n> We are on the mission to contribute to the growth and success of student entrepreneurs through active collaboration, access to an extensive network, and monetary support, while building a mutual learning relationship. \n\n### Vision\n\n> Our vision is to become the first contact for student entrepreneurs and a vital part of promoting student-led startups in the Twente region. \n\n![DSIF Join the team](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/elementor/thumbs/DSIF-recruitment-1-osr6pqf91s5a0hp3ypktuij2aepbuy8t7380u3qjgg.png \"DSIF recruitment\") \n\n## We are more than just an investment fund!\n\n![Guidance](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/elementor/thumbs/Guidance-p2ioacign93xkhpsv4ml7ywychuz85petbq17y4v6w.png \"Guidance\")\n\n### Guidance\n\nNext to financing, we offer young entrepreneurs guidance & appropriate feedback which can help to move start-up ideas to the next level. Professional advice helps any young entrepreneur to make a sensible decision about reaching their business goal. We want to share our knowledge and experience to help students avoid unnecessary mistakes on their journey to a successful startup.\n\n![Support](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/elementor/thumbs/Support-p2ioay4r0fxiziuecvz0bbgk0cwf5738kaq79b8t7s.png \"Support\")\n\n### Support\n\nWe support our portfolio start-ups in every step on their way to success by sharing our knowledge, experience, and advice from top-notch professionals from our network. We want to help the start-ups as much as possible and support them after the investment is done, too. We stay actively involved with the start-ups to monitor progress and offer support with the legal side of the business.\n\n![Guidance](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/elementor/thumbs/Guidance-p2ioacign93xkhpsv4ml7ywychuz85petbq17y4v6w.png \"Guidance\")\n\n### Network\n\nThe DSIF members participate in all kinds of networking events where we get access to a large professional network. Currently, the network of our partners consists of numerous companies and organizations (Novel-T, Hive01, Saxion Centre for Entrepreneurship, UT Challenge, Golden Egg Check, Incubase) that can help student entrepreneurs. We are in an ideal position to connect student entrepreneurs to companies and organizations.\n\n![Investment](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/elementor/thumbs/Investment-p2iobjr1dmr4ejyzunbfeo05o7xv28h2b9qdaocr8o.png \"Investment\")\n\n### Investment\n\nDSIF invests in startups created by bachelor, master, PhD students or recent graduates from the University of Twente or Saxion University of Applied Sciences. We invest from €5.000 to €10.000 in startups from various fields that could benefit society. \n\n## [Start your venture in 4 easy steps](https://www.dsif.nl/home/apply-for-funding/)\n\n[![Dutch Student Investment Fund One-pager](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Step-0.png)](https://www.dsif.nl/how-to-fundraise-start-up-one-pager-guideline/)\n\n[1 Send your one-pager](https://www.dsif.nl/how-to-fundraise-start-up-one-pager-guideline/)\n\nExplain your idea in one pager and send it over to us, we love ideas.\n\n![Dutch Student Investment Fund Business plan](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Step-2.png)\n\n2  \nSend your business plan\n\nWhen we like what we see we will ask you for a business plan.\n\n![Dutch Student Investment Fund Pitch](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Step-3.png)\n\n3  \nPitch your  \nidea\n\nWhen that is solid we will invite you to pitch to our board.\n\n![Dutch Student Investment Fund Deal](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Step-4-1-1024x778.png)\n\n4  \nMake a  \ndeal\n\nWhen the pitch is successful we will start the due-diligence process and make a deal!\n\n[ Learn More ](https://www.dsif.nl/home/for-founders/#Investment) \n\n## Portfolio of our investment fund\n\n![Dutch Student Investment FUnd x LoCoMoGo](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/Locomogo-Logo-1024x331.png) \n\n**[LoCoMoGo](https://www.locomogo.com/)** is the toy train that teaches children coding through play. We believe _every_ child should have the opportunity to learn coding, but above all, that a child should have fun.\n\n[ Learn more ](https://www.locomogo.com/) \n\n![Clairify - logo transparent](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/Clairify-logo-transparent.png) \n\n[**Clairify’s**](https://clairify.io/en/) smart sensors that detect indoor air quality (IAQ) and thermal comfort in offices, schools, and public buildings. The advanced data analysis provides asset and facility managers insights to help improve people’s well-being, productivity and prevent illness. The start-up is on the mission to improve buildings’ climate and comfort with its innovative technology.\n\n[ Learn more ](https://clairify.io/en/) \n\n[ ![](https://www.dsif.nl/wp-content/uploads/2022/12/LoopTas_logo.png) ](https://looptas.nl/) \n\n[**LoopTas**](https://looptas.nl/) develops innovative reusable shopping bags to tackle one of the world’s most serious problems: plastic waste. By giving out rewards to consumers after every reuse, LoopTas makes it easy and affordable for consumers to follow a more sustainable lifestyle. \n\n[ Learn more ](https://looptas.nl/) \n\nOur next investment can be in your own innovative startup. Whether you just have an idea and need some help shaping it, or you’ve been working for a while on your startup and you have a team. Drop us a line!\n\n[ Apply now ](https://www.dsif.nl/apply-for-funding/) \n\n## Testimonials\n\n “Partnering up with DSIF enabled LoCoMoGo to have a great start. and have backed over 45 companies\n\nWe have been actively involved in shaping the future of our portfolio companies\n\n[See all portfolio companies](/portfolio)\n\n## Our investment criteria\n\nSectors:\n\nBusiness Technology (HR & Payroll, Tax & Accounting, Regulatory, Legal & Compliance, Business Process Automation ) Finance Technology (Insurance, Payments, Banking & Wealth) \n\nStage:\n\nAt least an ARR of €2 million and profitable with our capital\n\nTarget Regions:\n\nEurope\n\nInvestment Ticket:\n\nInitial €5-15 Million (up to €50m with our investors investing in a Co-invest vehicle)\n\nBusiness Model:\n\nHigh Gross Margin, Technology led and capital efficient\n\nTeam:\n\nExceptional Founders & Management Team\n\nProduct Market Fit:\n\nProven product market fit with strong unit economics\n\nEquity Stake:\n\nSignificant Minority through growth capital, secondaries/minority buyout.\n\n## Read our latest posts\n\n[Research27 March 2025Market Pulse - AI-Fueled ](https://www.linkedin.com/company/rotterdam-port-fund)\n\n[](/news/main/elektrificatie-scheepvaart-ligt-op-schema-met-investering-van-4-miljoen-in-est-floattech-24330) \n\n[Elektrificatie scheepvaart ligt op schema met investering van € 4 miljoen in EST-Floattech](/news/main/elektrificatie-scheepvaart-ligt-op-schema-met-investering-van-4-miljoen-in-est-floattech-24330) \n\nOntwikkelaar van maritieme batterijsystemen EST-Floattech ontvangt een investering van 4 miljoen euro van Energy Transition Fund Rotterdam en bestaande aandeelhouders Rotterdam Port Fund, PDENH, Ponooc en Yard Energy. Dit maakte Chantal Zeegers, wethouder Klimaat, Bouwen en Wonen van de gemeente Rotterdam, bekend. Het Energietransitiefonds Rotterdam is het investeringsfonds van de gemeente Rotterdam.\n\n[Lees meer](/news/main/elektrificatie-scheepvaart-ligt-op-schema-met-investering-van-4-miljoen-in-est-floattech-24330)\n\n* [ Elektrificatie scheepvaart ligt op schema met investering van € 4 miljoen in EST-Floattech ](#)  \n[ Elektrificatie scheepvaart ligt op schema met investering van € 4 miljoen in EST-Floattech ](#)\n* [ Zo ziet de stofbestrijding van Wuvio eruit ](#)  \n[ Zo ziet de stofbestrijding van Wuvio eruit ](#)\n* [ Investering ter ondersteuning groeiambities Van Aalst ](#)  \n[ Investering ter ondersteuning groeiambities Van Aalst ](#)\n* [ McNetiq introduceert magnetische leidingsteunen ](#)  \n[ McNetiq introduceert magnetische leidingsteunen ](#)\n* [ Tagpoint ontwikkelt veiligheidstrainingen voor autoherstelschadebranche ](#)  \n[ Tagpoint ontwikkelt veiligheidstrainingen voor autoherstelschadebranche ](#)\n\n# Nieuws\n\n* R  \n[](/news/main/elektrificatie-scheepvaart-ligt-op-schema-met-investering-van-4-miljoen-in-est-floattech-24330)  \nNews  \n#### [Elektrificatie scheepvaart ligt op schema met investering van € 4 miljoen in EST-Floattech](/news/main/elektrificatie-scheepvaart-ligt-op-schema-met-investering-van-4-miljoen-in-est-floattech-24330)  \n\" 12:09 27/02/2024  \n Ontwikkelaar van maritieme batterijsystemen EST-Floattech ontvangt een investering van 4 miljoen euro van Energy Transition Fund Rotterdam en bestaande aandeelhouders Rotterdam Port Fund, PDENH, Ponooc en Yard Energy. Dit maakte Chantal Zeegers, wethouder Klimaat, Bouwen en Wonen van de gemeente Rotterdam, bekend. Het Energietransitiefonds Rotterdam is het investeringsfonds van de gemeente Rotterdam.\n* R  \n[](/news/main/rotterdam-port-fund-verkoopt-belang-in-nordic-booster-aan-akershus-energi-24317)  \nNews  \n#### [Rotterdam Port Fund verkoopt belang in Nordic Booster aan Akershus Energi](/news/main/rotterdam-port-fund-verkoopt-belang-in-nordic-booster-aan-akershus-energi-24317)  \n\" 11:24 13/02/2024  \n Februari 2024: RPF en zijn Nederlandse mede-investeerders Ponooc, Yard Energy Transition Fund I en PDENH hebben hun belang van 40% in Nordic Booster verkocht aan Akershus Energi, een gerenommeerd Noors energieconcern.\n* R  \n[](/news/main/est-floattech-lanceert-nieuw-product-24047)  \nNews  \n#### [EST-Floattech lanceert nieuw product](/news/main/est-floattech-lanceert-nieuw-product-24047)  \n\" 15:55 20/04/2023  \n Portfoliobedrijf EST-Floattech heeft op 13 april een nieuw product gelanceerd: de Octopus series batterij. De nieuwe productielijn werd geopend door Europarlementariër Caroline Nagtegaal-Van Doorn. Met de Octopus series kan EST-Floattech inspelen op de vraag van de maritieme sector naar efficiëntere batterijsystemen en een grote stap voorwaarts maken naar een emissievrije maritieme industrie.\n\nMijn postsFan posts\n\n[\\[](#prev)\n\n* [](/media?mediaId=27709857)  \n### RotterdamPortFund  \n@RotterdamPortFund  \nSteigeranker van McNetiq  \n[](/media?mediaId=27467398)  \n###
